## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / kinetic ODE modeling)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is a reaction-rate expression (time derivative of concentration), so the task is to infer a kinetic rate law for species A in an ODE dA/dt = f(t, A). With only (t, A) available, typical structures include zero/first/second-order consumption, generalized power-law kinetics, equilibrium relaxation, inhibition/saturation terms, and non-autonomous (time-varying) rate constants.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (rate independent of A; surface/photochemical zero-order regime)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive-like, many elementary decompositions)
- Relaxation to equilibrium (linear driving force): dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to steady state A=c1)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular with identical reactants or pseudo-second-order)
- General n-th order rate law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical power-law kinetics)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-form kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating growth limited by finite capacity/precursor)
- Production plus decay (source-sink): dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant feed/formation with first-order loss; e.g., CSTR with constant inflow term)
- Inhibition / saturation (self-inhibiting): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (rate increases then saturates; product inhibition / limited active sites)
- Sublinear (diffusion/heterogeneous-limited) uptake: dA_dt = -c0 * Abs(A)**c1 (0<c1<1 often indicates transport-limited effective kinetics)
- Reversible-like net rate toward a capacity: dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) - c2 * A (net formation from reservoir c1 with loss proportional to A)
- Time-varying first-order (deactivation/aging): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (effective rate constant decays over time)
- Periodic forcing (light/temperature cycling proxy): dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (externally modulated first-order kinetics; requires c1 to keep net positive prefactor)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If dA_dt is always negative and proportional to A, a first-order decay mechanism is likely; straight lines in d(ln A)/dt vs constant correspond to this structure.
- If dA_dt is approximately constant over a wide A range, a zero-order regime is suggested (surface-limited, catalyst-saturated, or constant flux).
- If the magnitude of dA_dt grows ~A^2, it indicates bimolecular/second-order kinetics; faster-than-exponential depletion at high A is typical.
- Presence of a stable fixed point A≈c1 (dA_dt changes sign around c1) suggests equilibrium/steady-state relaxation terms like -(A-c1) or A*(c1-A).
- Rational forms like A/(A+c1) indicate saturation or inhibition due to finite sites/active catalyst; rate becomes insensitive to A at large A.
- Sublinear power (A**c with 0<c<1) is a common signature of transport or heterogeneous limitations where effective reaction order drops.
- Explicit time dependence in the prefactor (e.g., exp(-c*t)) often encodes catalyst deactivation, reagent exhaustion not represented as a state, or changing external conditions.
- Sinusoidal dependence on t is a proxy for periodic forcing (illumination cycles, pulsed feed, temperature cycling) producing oscillatory rate modulation.
- A constant source term (+c0) combined with first-order loss (-c1*A) typically yields approach to a nonzero steady concentration (balance of production and decay).

============================================================

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK2)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_w*cos(log(A + c2))
Candidate formulas: 51

GT is the fixed function (independent of `t`):
\[
f(A)= -0.19494483384724354\,A \;+\; 0.24819026785686927\;\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (possibly after setting some candidate constants to 0) to produce **(i)** a linear-in-\(A\) term and **(ii)** a cosine of a **logarithm of an affine function of \(A\)**, with **no remaining \(t\)-dependence**, on some plausible continuous domain (e.g. \(A>-1\) so \(\log(A+1)\) is defined).

Below, I check each candidate for whether it can be tuned to exactly \(-kA + m\cos(\log(A+1))\) (with the specific fixed GT coefficients), allowing domain restrictions like \(A\ge 0\) to remove `Abs(A)`.

---

### 1. `A**2 + A*c0 + c1*exp(A*c2) + c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + c6 + c7*cos(c8*exp(A*c9))`
Has unavoidable `A**2` term (fixed coefficient 1). Cannot remove it with parameters. Not match.

### 2. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5 + c6*t + c7*log(c8*Abs(A) + 1)))`
Cos(log(.)) not present; has `exp(sin(...))`. Also `log(c8*Abs(A)+1)` is inside a sine inside an exp, not a cosine of log. Not match.

### 3. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*Abs(A)) + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5) + c6 + Abs(A)`
To remove non-GT parts: set `c1=0`, `c3=0`, but then left with linear + `Abs(A)` + constant. `Abs(A)` cannot be removed (coefficient 1). Not match.

### 4. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6*log(c7*Abs(A) + 1) + c8)) + Abs(A)`
Again has `Abs(A)` with coefficient 1 (cannot be zeroed). Not match.

### 5. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*Abs(A)**c3 + c4*log(c5*t + 1)`
To match GT must remove `t` term: set `c4=0`. Remove `A^2`: set `c0=0`. Then left with linear + power of `Abs(A)`; cannot become cosine(log(A+1)). Not match.

### 6. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2`
Pure affine in A; cannot create cosine(log(A+1)). Not match.

### 7. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4`
To remove `t`, set `c2=0` (or `c3=0` gives constant but still no cosine(log)). No cosine(log). Not match.

### 8. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*Abs(A)**c3 + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 9. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + Abs(A)**c3 + c4*t/A**5`
Has explicit `t` unless `c4=0`. Then polynomial/power only; no cosine(log). Not match.

### 10. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*t/(A*c4 + c5) + c6/(A*c4 + c5)`
Remove `t` by `c3=0`. Still rational term `c6/(A*c4+c5)`; can set `c6=0` too, leaving affine only. No cosine(log). Not match.

### 11. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(A*c4)*cos(c5*t)`
To remove `t` dependence, either `c3=0` (kills cosine entirely) or force `cos(c5*t)` constant for all t (only possible if `c5=0`, then cos=1). If `c5=0`, term becomes `c3*exp(A*c4)` (not cosine(log)). Not match.

### 12. `A*c0 + A*c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + A + c4/(A + c5) + c6*Abs(A)**c7`
Has `A` with fixed coefficient 1 plus other terms; cannot produce cosine(log(A+1)). Not match.

### 13. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2) + c3*Abs(A)**c4 + c5*Max(0, c6 - t)`
Has `t` via `Max`; can set `c5=0`. Still no cosine(log). Not match.

### 14. `A*c0*(c1 + t)**c2 + A + A**c3*c4/(A**c3 + c5) + c6/(A + c7) + c8*Abs(A)**c9`
Has fixed `+A` term; also no cosine(log). Not match.

### 15. `A*c0 + c1*exp(c2*t)*sin(c3*t + c4)*Abs(A)**c5 + Abs(A)**c6`
No cosine(log); also `Abs(A)**c6` unavoidable unless choose domain? But coefficient is 1, cannot remove. Not match.

### 16. `A**2 + A*c0 + c1*exp(A*c2) + c3 + c4*cos(c5*exp(A*c6))`
Has unavoidable `A**2` term. Not match.

### 17. `c0*sin(A*c1 + c2)`
Sine of linear A, not cosine of log(A+1). Not match.

### 18. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*log(c4*t + 1)*log(c5*Abs(A) + 1) + Abs(A)`
Has `Abs(A)` with coefficient 1 (cannot remove). Not match.

### 19. `A + c0/(c1 + Abs(A)**c2) + c3*Abs(A)**c4 + c5/A`
Has fixed `A` coefficient 1; GT has coefficient -0.1949 plus cosine(log). Not match.

### 20. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2 + Abs(A)**c3`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 21. Rational combination of powers over `(A + c1)` plus `Abs(A)**...` terms
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 22. `A**2*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + A**c3`
No cosine(log); also `t` unless `c0=0` or `c1=0`. Still no cosine(log). Not match.

### 23. `A**2*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + Abs(A)**c3`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 24. `A*c0/(A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c2*t)) + A**c4*c5 + c6*log(A*c7 + 1)`
This has a `log(A*c7+1)` term (promising), but GT needs `cos(log(A+1))`, i.e., cosine *of* a log, not a linear combination including a log. Candidate has no cosine around the log. Not match.

### 25. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 26. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*Max(0, A + c3) + c4*t/(A*c5 + c6) + c7/(A*c5 + c6)`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 27. Contains `log(c6*exp(c7*t)*Abs(A)**c8 + 1)` plus other rational/power terms
Again only `log(...)`, not `cos(log(...))`. Not match.

### 28. `c0 + c1*cos(A*c2) + c3*exp(c4*t)`
Cosine of linear A, not cosine of log(A+1). Also `t` unless `c3=0`. Not match.

### 29. `A*c0/(A + c1) + A + A**c2*c3 + c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6*Abs(A)**c7`
Has `log(A*c5+1)` but not `cos(log(...))`; also fixed `+A`. Not match.

### 30. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*t + Abs(A)**c4`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 44. `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*Abs(A) + 1) + c6)`
This has `sin( c4*log(c5*Abs(A)+1)+c6 )`, which is close in *structure* to `cos(log(A+1))` (since `cos(x)=sin(x+pi/2)`), but:
- It is **sine of log of (c5*Abs(A)+1)**, not cosine of log(A+1) unless we can set `c5=1` and restrict domain `A>=0` so `Abs(A)=A`. That part is fine.
- However GT also has a **linear term** `-0.1949*A`. Candidate’s non-sine part is `A**c0*c1 + c2`, i.e., a power term. We could set `c0=1` to make it linear `c1*A`, and set `c2=0`. Then candidate becomes `c1*A + c3*sin(c4*log(A+1)+c6)`.
Now can we match exactly?
  - Need `c1 = -0.19494483384724354`.
  - Need sine to equal `0.24819026785686927*cos(log(A+1))`.
    Use identity: `cos(u)=sin(u+pi/2)`. So set:
    - `c4 = 1` (match `log(A+1)` scaling),
    - `c6 = pi/2` (phase shift),
    - `c3 = 0.24819026785686927`,
    - and domain condition `A>=0` (or more generally `A>-1` and also ensure `Abs(A)=A` if using that; easiest is `A>=0`).
Also must ensure no extra scaling `_w` is needed: GT already has `0.24819*cos(log(A+1))` (the `_w` has been absorbed into the numeric coefficient), so we just match that coefficient.
Thus candidate 44 **can** be made equivalent to GT on domain `A>=0` (or any domain where `Abs(A)=A` and `A>-1`).

So 44 is a valid match.

### 45. `A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3) + c4 + c5*t + Abs(A)`
Has `Abs(A)` with coefficient 1. Not match.

### 46. `A*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + c3*Abs(A)**c4 + c5/(A*c1 + c2)`
No cosine(log). Not match.

### 47. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + Abs(A)**c3`
No cosine(log). Not match.

No cosine(log). Not match.

### 50. `A + c0/(A + c1) + c2*Abs(A)**c3 + c4/(c5*exp(c6*t) + 1)`
Fixed `+A`. Not match.

### 51. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2 + c3*log(A*c4 + 1)`
No cosine(log). Not match.

A concrete parameterization for candidate **44** that matches GT on domain **A ≥ 0**:
- `c0 = 1`
- `c1 = -0.19494483384724354`
- `c2 = 0`
- `c3 = 0.24819026785686927`
- `c4 = 1`
- `c5 = 1`
- `c6 = π/2` (≈ 1.5707963267948966)

Then:
\[
A^{1}c1 + c3\sin(\log(A+1)+\pi/2)= -0.1949448A + 0.2481903\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
